    üéñ From January 1, Heroes of Ukraine and holders of orders will receive monthly cash payments

    On January 1, 2023, the Law of Ukraine came into force, which establishes monthly payments of financial assistance to people who have been awarded the title of Hero of Ukraine with the award of the Order of the Golden Star, Knights of the Order of Bohdan Khmelnytsky and Knights of the Order "For Courage".

    Monthly payment of financial assistance is introduced:
    ‚ñ™Ô∏è in the amount of three minimum wages established on January 1 of the calendar year - to persons who have been awarded the title of Hero of Ukraine with the award of the Order of the Golden Star (today it is UAH 20,100);
    ‚ñ™Ô∏èin the amount of two minimum wages - knights of the Order of Bohdan Khmelnytsky of three degrees (UAH 13,400);

    ‚ñ™Ô∏èin the amount of one minimum wage - to holders of the Order "For Courage" of three degrees (full holders) (UAH 6,700).

    ‚ñ™Ô∏èIn addition, a monthly payment of financial assistance is established in the amount of three to one (per month per family) of the minimum wage to family members of deceased or posthumously awarded persons who were awarded the title of Hero of Ukraine with the award of the Order of the Golden Star, Knights of the Order of Bohdan Khmelnytsky of three degrees (full knights) and holders of the Order "For Courage" of three degrees (full knights).

    Ukraine has probably managed to establish its own production of 152-mm shells, and they are already at the front.

    OSINT researchers from Ukraine Weapons Tracker came to this conclusion after analyzing several photos from the frontline.

    Serhiy Khrypun, a resident of Orikhiv village, Zaporizhzhya region, was abducted by Russians on March 24. He worked as a security guard at the farm "Ukrlan" in the village of Nove. On that day, Serhiy was at work with his colleagues.

    "We have not seen my father since February 22, that is, since he went to work in the village of Nove. After the beginning of the war, the Russians immediately occupied the village where the company was located. So he found himself under occupation without any documents", - Yulia said.

    According to her, the relatives tried to take Serhiy Khrypun out of the occupied village for a month. But due to the lack of a passport, they did not want to let him through the Ukrainian checkpoint.

    SBU CI officers detained another enemy accomplice during a multi-stage special operation in western Ukraine.

    It was a resident of Donetsk region, who after the beginning of full-scale invasion passed information to the representative of terrorist organization.

    Since the beginning of the war he collected intelligence on the location and movement of the units of the Ukrainian Defence Forces in the Liman direction. Later, the traitor moved to Lviv region, where he continued his reconnaissance and subversive activities.

    Under the guise of an internally displaced person, he settled near one of the energy facilities. The man continued collecting information for the enemy special service.

    However, the SBU officers exposed the enemy's accomplice on attempts to covertly collect and transfer information through a "liaison" in the ranks of the "DNR" terrorist groups.

    During the operative actions, the SBU officers seized a mobile phone with correspondence with the enemy.

    Based on the collected evidence, the SBU investigators served him a notice of suspicion of committing the crime.

    The court imposed on him a measure of restraint in the form of detention without the right to be released on bail.

    The special operation was conducted by the SBU officers in Lviv region under the procedural supervision of the Regional Prosecutor's Office.

    The scandalous president of FC "Ingulets" got into the "Peacemaker" database

    The president of FC Ingulets, a businessman-agrarian and a deputy of the Petrovsky district council Alexander Povoroznyuk appeared in the "Mirotvorets" database. He is accused of conscious looting of Ukraine. The corresponding map with the accusations appeared on the website Myrotvorets.center.

    "Marauder. Thief. Conscious actions aimed at plundering Ukraine. He candidly confessed that he had plundered the state for a long time, bragging that he had made his fortune with it," the Peacemaker website states.

    It is also noted that Povoroznyuk has at least three convictions, including one for theft of state property.

    On the eve Povoroznyuk admitted that he never stole from concrete people, but only from the abstract state of Ukraine. This, according to his version, is called "I made my own capital".

    Alexander Povoroznyuk is a scandalously known businessman-agrarian. General Director of LLC "Agrofirma Pyatihatska", president of FC "Ingulets". In 2009-2010 - president of FC "Desna". Deputy of Petrovsky district council since 2010. After the full-scale invasion of russia into Ukraine, he recorded a video appeal to the President of Ukraine Volodymyr Zelenski, which went viral after a DJ mix was recorded on it.

    Peacemaker is a center for investigating signs of crimes against Ukraine's national security, peace, human security and international law. A Ukrainian website and public organization that publishes data about people the authors of the site consider enemies of Ukraine. It is an independent non-governmental organization. The site was created in December 2014 by Ukrainian politician and activist Heorhiy Tuka.

    TRANSLATION :
    üè† How can IDPs join the queue for temporary housing?

    According to the Resolution of the Cabinet of Ministers, internally displaced persons can join the queue for temporary housing. Housing from the fund at the place of actual residence / stay within the territory of the authorized bodies is provided to IDPs and their family members free of charge and is determined in the amount of at least 6 square meters per person, Finance writes.

    üìù Citizens who were forced to move to other regions of Ukraine must submit an application for registration of persons in need of housing for temporary residence. The application is submitted to the authorized body within the territory of which they are registered in the Unified Information Database on IDPs.

    The application shall be accompanied by:
    ‚Üí copies of identity documents confirming the citizenship of Ukraine;
    ‚Üí copy of the internally displaced person's certificate of registration in the Unified Information Database on IDPs and copies of relevant certificates of family members (if any);
    ‚Üí copies of documents issued by the civil registry office or court confirming the kinship of the applicant and all members of his/her family (birth certificate, marriage certificate, certificate of guardian or custodian, etc;)
    ‚Üí copy of the registration number of the taxpayer's account card;
    ‚Üí copies of documents confirming the grounds for priority in providing IDPs with housing from the fund (the fact of destruction or damage to housing, which led to the impossibility of its intended use, is confirmed by a personal statement of the applicant and his family members).

    After submitting the application, a decision is made within one working day to register IDPs as citizens in need of housing for temporary residence or to refuse to register them.

    What will be the prices for apartments in Kyiv in 2023: expert forecast

    In 2022, real estate prices in Kyiv decreased by about 15-20%, but in 2023 the cost will not fall. Prices are likely to remain at the current level for the next six months. However, the situation will be influenced by the news from the front.

    This was told by the President of the Association of Realtors of Ukraine Yuriy Pita. According to him, there is a demand for apartments in the capital, but many people are still in no hurry to buy real estate, as the risks due to the war still remain.

    "We will rely on the trends of the last few months - November-December - because the market has basically stabilized. There are no significant shifts in the direction of increase or decrease in value. In 2022, prices fell by about 15-20%, this is since the beginning of the war. They are not continuing their fall, so prices will be at this level. They have fallen to a certain level and will remain so. But, again, much will depend on the situation in the country as a whole," the expert explained.

    Pita added: if there are successes on the front, then the real estate market will also react quite actively. In addition, compensation to Ukrainians who lost their homes will have a positive impact on the situation.

    "We hope that housing compensation programs will be launched for those who have lost their homes. This will also affect the market. There will be, perhaps, some monetary compensation or square meters. And the apartments on the market will be searched for somewhere, bought, transferred to those who suffered.

    So, such trends will be at least six months, and then we will see what will happen next. That is, no significant changes in prices are not expected," - the expert concluded.
